95632db910efd05569c15c69d38e34a71372062a|2013-12-18|Kristian Spangsege|Eliminate warnings relating to `MAX_JLONG`. First warning was eliminated by add suffix `LL` to the constant. This is necessary becuase `long long` is the smallest and only type that ANSI guarantees is 64 bits. Likewise, `MAX_JINT` must have an `L` suffix, because `long` is the smallest type that ANSI guarantees is 32 bits. The second and last warning was removed by using `util::int_less_than_or_equal()` (a utility function created precisely for this purpose).
